Hankou dispatch. The Bandit Suppression Headquarters of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Provinces decided to establish a Rural Financial Relief Office and appointed Guo Waifeng as the director. Guo arrived in Hankou from Nanjing on the 16th. Due to Commander-in-Chief Chiang's urging, he organized and established the office in the Ningbo Guild Hall on the 21st. Guo immediately announced his assumption of office and appointed the office's staff, including Secretary Chen Guoquan, staff members Jin Xueteng, Cheng Weijia, Liu Ruxiang, Ling Jingshan, Wang Xianggui, Wei Junming, Yang Heqing, seven people, and several clerks and secretaries. Cheng Weijia was appointed as the director of the General Affairs Group, Liu Ruxiang as the director of the Guidance Group, Ling Jingshan as the director of the Audit Group, and Jin Xueteng as the assistant secretary. Before Chen Guoquan arrives, Jin Xueteng will temporarily act as the secretary. According to Guo, after I arrived in Hankou on the 16th, I was ordered by Commander-in-Chief Chiang to take office as soon as possible, because the areas with heavy bandit disasters urgently need to be rescued in order to recover. This time, the League of Nations agricultural experts went to central Hubei for inspection. When they came to Hankou, they talked about the fact that there were no耕牛 (oxen) within hundreds of miles in central Hubei, and there was also a lack of seeds. Many farmers used reed sheds to avoid the cold, which was extremely miserable. The establishment of this office is to assist the development of rural cooperatives, so that the rural economy can gradually recover. In terms of responsibilities, emphasis is placed on guidance and auditing. However, the disaster-stricken area in one province is very large, and the restoration of rural areas requires manpower and financial resources to advance at the same time to be effective. Now the headquarters has a rural cooperative instructor training center in Wuchang, which is organized by Wen Qun. The first batch of 50 students will graduate in a week and will soon set off to various places to work in the field. The office will first start a pilot rural cooperative in Hubei Province and then promote it to Henan and Anhui provinces. When the graduates of the training center set off, the guidance group of the office will also send people to guide them. As for the funding, Commander-in-Chief Chiang has telegraphed the provinces and cities to donate, and he thinks there will be good results soon. The headquarters will also find a way to lend 1 million yuan from the banking industry for the purpose of rescuing rural circulating capital. (October 21)

Fuzhou Newspapers Suspended Publication for Three Days

▲ Due to Interference by the Municipal Public Security Bureau in Records

Fuzhou dispatch. After Qiu Zhaochen, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, shot and killed Zheng Weixin, the representative of the petitioning delegation of the People's Association for Eliminating Inferiority, his mother, Zheng Lin, issued a crying appeal, accusing Qiu of indiscriminate killing of innocent young people and suppressing the patriotic movement, and requesting assistance from all sectors. Zheng was originally a teacher at Duqing Elementary School. Huang Zhanyun, the chairman of the school's board of directors, also submitted a report to the provincial government's Pacification Commissioner's Office, requesting a thorough investigation to maintain justice and protect human rights. The local newspapers held a joint meeting on the morning of the 16th and decided to unanimously publish Huang's original report. When Qiu Zhaochen heard the news, he sent people to the newspapers in the afternoon to request that they not be published, but he was rejected by the newspapers. At 12:00 p.m. that night, the Municipal Public Security Bureau suddenly dispatched many police officers to the Qiushi Newspaper Office, claiming that they were acting on the order of the Pacification Commissioner's Office. The newspaper's publication of the news that Zhang Yan's brigade was heading to Yanping had leaked military secrets and violated Article 21 of the Publishing Law. It should be punished by suspending publication for three days as a warning. The newspaper then complied with the order and suspended publication from the 17th. In order to express sympathy for the Qiushi Newspaper, the other newspapers convened a meeting in the afternoon and decided that, with the exception of the Min Guo Daily, which was run by the Provincial Party Department, they would also voluntarily suspend publication for three days from the 18th and issued a declaration, which read, "Our newspapers deeply feel that in the past ten days, we have had many concerns in terms of speech, and it is difficult to write truthfully about events in terms of records. Even the Qiushi Daily published certain news, which was mostly similar to what other newspapers in the city had published, but the newspaper alone was held responsible and ordered to suspend publication for three days. The punishment has no standard and is unfair. How can the newspapers feel safe? We have no choice but to voluntarily suspend publication for three days in order to promote a strong sense of reflection. We hereby announce this in the hope that you will understand." It was also agreed that after resuming publication, they would uniformly publish a notice on the newspaper, "Under orders, military news is not allowed to be published. We hope that readers will understand." However, on the afternoon of the 18th, the Public Security Bureau sent an inspection team to arrest Xia Yuchou, the editor-in-chief of the Chao Bao, and Lin Yipeng, the general manager of the Xiandai Daily. Fortunately, Xia and Lin heard the news and avoided it, so they were not arrested. It is now reported that the authorities are also dissatisfied with Qiu's actions in recent days. After the provincial government received Huang Zhanyun's complaint, it ordered Qiu Zhaochen to submit a report to the provincial government on the circumstances of the shooting and killing of Zheng Weixin on that day, along with the reactionary evidence obtained, for verification. The Pacification Commissioner's Office has considered withdrawing Qiu Zhaochen and requesting the provincial government to reappoint Tian Guozhang, the former commander of the 61st Division, as the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. (November 19)

Reasons for Economic Decline in Shandong Province

▲Cheap Grain Hurts Farmers, Rural Areas Bankrupt

▲Foreign Goods Flood the Market, National Products Decline

▲Northeast Falls, Income Sharply Decreases

Jinan Correspondence: This province has had a bumper grain harvest this year, the best in decades, but the economic decline and the people's hardship are also the worst in decades. The average middle-class farmer in rural areas is in danger of bankruptcy. Although the grain harvest is abundant, there are few buyers, the price is extremely low, and labor is very expensive, resulting in high expenses and low income. This has led to the phenomenon of cheap grain hurting farmers. After entering winter, prices of all goods have fallen, but sales are still sluggish, and the purchasing power of society is particularly weak. According to Director Wang Fangting of the Department of Industry, the phenomenon of cheap grain hurting farmers is widespread throughout the country this year. Examining the causes, they are none other than the three basic necessities of life: clothing, food, and shelter. Our people prefer to use foreign goods, and except for food, almost everything else is a market for foreign goods. For example, the Qingdao area is now full of American flour and Japanese coal. Shandong's only indigenous food product, wheat, and fuel such as Boshan coal, are also greatly affected. Other goods such as cotton yarn, ironware, lumber, and daily necessities are also all foreign goods. Countless amounts of money are flowing out to foreign countries like trickles of water, resulting in the current situation of poor people and exhausted wealth. The only way for the Department of Industry to remedy this is to promote the improvement of national products, increase production, and replace foreign goods as a fundamental plan. The current measures include: ㈠ Expanding spinning. The northwest region of this province is a major cotton-producing area. However, although the cotton produced is abundant, there are only two spinning mills, Lufeng in Jinan and Huaxin in Qingdao. A new company, Tongyi, has been organized in Jinan, but it has not yet started operations. A large amount of cotton is thus used by foreign yarn factories to absorb our country's money. Therefore, the spinning industry must be actively expanded. However, it is easy to celebrate success with the people, but difficult to plan the beginning with them. Relying solely on persuasion has little effect. It is decided that next year, each county will be forced to convene commercial and private shareholders to establish yarn factories. At least two should be established first. ㈡ Supporting enterprises. The industry in this province is still in its infancy. There are too few factories. The Department of Industry protects and supports enterprises, providing assistance and guidance to new ones, and assisting existing ones to develop, striving to prevent their closure. The department has also established a model pottery factory in Boshan. Since its establishment, it has produced many products, and Japanese porcelain has gradually decreased by 20-30%. ㈢ Cultivating timber. Although this province has many mountains, they are all barren and do not produce timber. All timber used is imported from the United States and the Northeast, and the amount of money flowing out is considerable. Now that the Northeast has fallen into Japanese hands, the Department of Industry is planning to expand afforestation and cultivate timber for future needs. However, it will take several years to see the benefits. ㈣ Promoting cotton planting and establishing cotton experimental farms to improve cotton production has been quite effective. According to surveys, the cotton production in this province this year is sufficient for the province's own use. ㈤ Civilian factories. The Department of Industry has been setting up civilian factories in various counties since last year to develop local industries and provide for the poor. Most of the 108 counties in the province have been established. Because cloth is most needed, weaving factories are the most numerous. In a few years, they may disappear from our market. ㈥ Rescuing the coal industry. Yixian Zhongxing on the Jinpu Railway, Zhangqiu, Zichuan, and Boshan on the Jiaoji Railway are the largest coal-producing areas in this province. In addition to supplying the province's own use, they can also be sold to Qingdao, Shanghai, Hankou, and other places. Boshan suffered a major flood this year, reducing production and increasing costs. Sales in Qingdao, Shanghai, and other places have also been seized by Japanese Fushun coal. Therefore, Yixian Zhongxing, with its larger capital, has suffered heavy losses, and the smaller coal mines in Boshan have closed down one after another. The Department of Industry is thus reducing coal surcharges on the one hand and planning to establish a Boshan power plant to supply electricity for mining, thereby reducing costs. The budget for the power plant requires 2.1 million yuan of capital, but after it is opened, it can earn 300,000 to 400,000 yuan per year. The shares are borne by the mine owners, and the benefits are shared. The cost of each mine will be reduced by a certain amount, and the price of coal will be lower, which should be able to compete with foreign coal, and so on.

According to a certain person in economic circles, although there are many reasons for the economic decline in Shandong this year, the fall of the Northeast is also the biggest reason. Many Shandong people go to the Northeast to cultivate every year. At the end of each year, they bring back the fruits of their year's hard work. The Jinpu and Jiaoji railways specially open small ticket cars for transportation. Postal remittances are also extremely busy. Although there are no statistics, it is probably no less than tens of millions of yuan. Last year, first there was the Wanbaoshan Incident, followed by the fall of the Northeast. Many Shandong people in Korea and the Northeast were expelled and returned. The postal service tried its best, but before the Northeast postal service was sealed, remittances from the Northeast had already disappeared. The Jinpu and Jiaoji railways only see refugees with emaciated faces, and no longer see Shandong people returning home with wealth. This is another major impact of the fall of the Northeast on Shandong province. (20th)

Jiangsu Province Levies Labor to Build the Nanjing-Jiangxi Railway

▲Can Be Fully Completed by March Next Year

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The Nanjing-Jiangxi Railway starts from Zhonghua Gate in Nanjing, passes through Andemen, Zilin Pass, Wucha Bridge, Lishui, Gaochun, and reaches Langxi in Anhui province. The section within Jiangsu province is 120 kilometers long. The section from Nanjing to Zilin Pass already had a military road built earlier. The engineering for the section from Wucha Bridge through Lishui to Gaochun was entrusted to Engineer Fu Guoshao by the Jiangsu Construction Department in July of this year, concurrently serving as the director of the Nanjing-Yixing section. He has completed the survey of the route, and an engineering office was established on September 1st to conduct detailed measurements. The bridge engineering has already started on October 15th and should be completed by the end of the year. The plan for levying labor to build the roadbed, as planned by the office, has been approved by the provincial government. Zhai Huan, secretary of the Construction Department, was appointed as the chief commissioner of the labor levy for the road, concurrently serving as the labor supervision commissioner for Gaochun County. Gao Suochen was appointed as the labor supervision commissioner for Jiangning County, and Kang Rongsen was appointed as the labor supervision commissioner for Lishui County. Yesterday, orders were issued to the officials to proceed to their posts and start work as soon as possible. The entire engineering for the road is scheduled to be completed by March of next year. (22nd)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

▲Bankruptcy Case of Songjiang Bank Opens for Trial. The bankruptcy case of Songjiang Bank, after the creditors formed a creditors' group and hired lawyers Qu Yue and Liu Zhimou to represent them in suing the bank's directors for responsible repayment, was heard by Judge Wang in court yesterday (21st) at 9:00 AM. The defendant directors Yan Shaxunyi and the special agent lawyer Tang Mingshi appeared in court. More than ten creditors, including Bo Guanlan, Wu Boyang, and Wang Muji, arrived. First, creditor Bo Guanlan stated that the case had been delayed for nine months and requested a swift judgment to protect the interests of the creditors. The creditors had come from afar to Songjiang, and the round trips had resulted in many losses. Then, Zhang Zuo, Liu Wu Boyang, and others made their requests in turn. The questioning continued until 12:00, but was not completed. The court continued to open at 2:00 PM. As a result of the dispute, because the director Zhang Sansheng had died and his property was not being managed, they requested a provisional attachment. Lawyer Sha argued that the person who would inherit from Zhang Sansheng, one of the directors, had not yet been determined. The so-called provisional attachment should first have the procedures corrected before the debate could begin. Then, Lawyer Qu delivered an eloquent argument, arguing that waiting until the seventh day after the funeral would still leave sixty days, and the third anniversary period. If another director also had the same situation, waiting in turn would mean that the creditors would never have hope of repayment. He requested that the debate be opened immediately and that the procedures be corrected afterwards. Lawyer Sha still opposed this. The judge ordered that the plaintiff correct the procedures before reopening the debate for review and approval.

Among the two thugs who unsuccessfully attempted to rob and then suddenly inflicted knife wounds in the evening, one was the person who had looked at the house that day. His face was recognized by Ni's wife. It is said that he claimed to work for a certain organization. The case has not yet been solved, and the public security authorities are strictly arresting the perpetrators.

Fengxian

▲Ancient Tomb Discovered at Murder Bridge. The tomb area near Murder Bridge, about three miles east of Nanqiao, was originally extremely desolate. Recently, farmers Wang Si, Li Shubing, and others were digging mud there to build a levee. When they dug about a foot below ground, they suddenly saw a stone slab. They gathered many people to remove the stone slab, and below it was a brick tomb. The surrounding wall feet were made of lime and glutinous rice flour, which was extremely hard. The inner and outer coffins inside the tomb had already decayed, but the two coffins were still intact and as new. When the coffin lids were opened, there were male and female corpses inside. The man wore a gauze hat with two wings on the side, a long-sleeved robe, and square-toed black boots. A round bronze mirror, as large as a bowl with bird-like patterns, was placed on his chest. The woman's upper body clothes were scattered and incomplete, but she still had a red skirt on her lower body. A square box containing four items such as wooden combs was placed next to her head, and they were not damp. Her pillow, which looked like a block of wood, was extremely soft, about three inches long and one foot wide, concave in the middle and convex on the outside, which was quite strange. The style of the two coffins was rectangular and made of four single-width boards nailed together, sounding like a bell when knocked. Those who knew recognized them as nanmu wood, worth ten thousand gold. However, there were no inscriptions in the tomb to verify the time, but judging from the clothes, they were probably figures from the Yuan or Ming dynasties. After learning about this, the township chief Liu Maoxing immediately reported it to the district office. The public security bureau sent Inspector Chen Jinfang to inspect the site yesterday, and it was confirmed to be true. At the same time, two empty coffins were found in Wang Si's house, so the official, in addition to notifying the township chief to temporarily guard the site, reported back to the bureau and district today to await further investigation.

▲Former Director of the Kunshan Construction Bureau Escorted to the Province for Interrogation. Wu Junyu, the former director of the Kunshan County Construction Bureau, embezzled more than 20,000 yuan in mu donations. After being reported by the county party headquarters, the county government arrested Wu, interrogated him, and imprisoned him for half a year. He has not yet been sentenced. Now the county government has received an order from the province to escort Wu to the province for interrogation. After receiving the order, County Chief Cheng dispatched police captain Luo Yanxiang yesterday morning to escort Wu by early train to the provincial office to await interrogation.

▲Strange Fetus. Zhang Xingsheng, a tailor who lived outside the West Gate, had a wife who had been pregnant for more than a year and had a large belly. The other day, she suddenly felt abdominal pain and was about to give birth. Xingsheng hurriedly called a midwife to his home to deliver the baby. By noon yesterday, two days and nights had passed, but the fetus had not yet been born. Zhang urgently invited Dr. Wang from Kunshan Hospital to use surgery to try to remove the fetus, but it had already died. Dr. Wang carefully examined the fetus and found it to be quite peculiar. The head was pointed like an olive, the genitals were born under the forehead, it had one eye on its face, no nose, a mouth as small as a yellow bean, and six fingers and toes on each hand and foot. Dr. Wang took it away as a specimen. When people heard about it, those who went to Kunshan Hospital to see it blocked the door. This is specially recorded for the study of physiologists.

Wuxi

▲Three Robbery Cases on Land and Water in One Night. Robbery cases are frequently heard during the winter prevention period, and the future of public security is particularly worrying. Tongyang Bridge outside the South Gate is lined with shops and is very prosperous. There is a public stove, and the owner is Chen Ada, who hires a group of friends to manage everything. Chen pulls a rickshaw for Qian Fenghao, the owner of the Dingchang Silk Factory. Opposite the public stove is the newly built school building of Xizhong Middle School, and both sides are workshops of the Dingchang Silk Factory. On the night before yesterday (21st) at around 7:00 PM, four robbers wearing black clothes and blue pants suddenly came to Chen Ada's public stove, holding weapons such as pistols and flashlights. They poured in and first grabbed Chen's wife, forbidding her from making a sound. One robber immediately forced Chen's wife to take off her gold ring and gold bracelet. The remaining robbers entered the room and searched it arbitrarily. After more than ten minutes, they roared out. After the robbers left the public stove, they reunited with several robbers who had been lying in ambush and broke into the nearby workshop at No. 35, robbing the home of Che Gushengfu, the chief manager of the Dingchang Silk Factory. At that time, Gu's wife and three or four young sisters were chatting and laughing in the room. After the robbers entered, they immediately took out guns and forbade them from making a sound, ordering them to take off the gold rings on their hands. Gu's wife and others had no choice but to let them rob them. They escaped with their loot at around 11:00 PM, and fired three shots as a show of force before leaving. Also, the Xichang night boat, fully loaded with goods, left Xichang at around 7:00 PM on the afternoon of the same day. The boat crew was pulling the boat along the shore, but when they passed near Gaoqiao, they suddenly encountered eight or nine robbers who rushed out of the mulberry fields, holding box cannons. They first grabbed the boat crew who were pulling the boat, ordered them to stop the boat, and then rushed onto the boat to search and rob at will. After about half an hour, they escaped with their loot. It is estimated that the goods robbed were worth more than 700 yuan.

Therefore, he has again sent a letter to Committee Member Shi Liangcai and Committee Member Zhang Gongquan of the National Economic Commission, asking them to appeal to the Ministry of Finance on his behalf.

Education News Highlights

Vice Minister Duan Talks About the Normal University Not Being Reorganized

Nanjing, 22nd Telegram. Vice Minister of Education Duan Xipeng talked about the reorganization of the Normal University, stating that the Ministry has not made any decisions. During July, Minister Zhu said that some people have recently advocated that the Normal University should only admit graduates of normal schools who are determined to become secondary school teachers to study for one year. Some people in the Ministry also advocated that the current system should be maintained, and that its courses and organization should all be suitable for the purpose of training teachers. It seems that rumors about the reorganization of the Normal University have arisen because of this. The Ministry believes that this issue is important and must be carefully studied. Therefore, there has never been any decision. What is the so-called cancellation? If the current system of the Normal University really needs reform, it cannot be cancelled simply because of disagreement from any party. In short, the current urgent task of the Normal University is to seriously reorganize the current situation and strive to make the curriculum and equipment suitable for the purpose of training secondary school teachers, so as to live up to the name of the Normal University. The rectification of the school's academic atmosphere is a matter that cannot be ignored. Those who truly love the Normal University should devote themselves to this.

National Central University Postpones Winter Vacation

▲Postponed to January 20th Next Year

Nanjing, 22nd Telegram. Central University decided to postpone the winter vacation to January 20th next year because the start of the semester was delayed due to student unrest and the teaching time for each student was uneven.

Ministry of Education Issues Standards for Kindergarten and Elementary School Curriculum (6)

Third, Key Operational Items for Each Academic Year (Continued)

Academic Year Category Key Items

Fifth and Sixth Academic Years

Habits The development of the following habits 1 to 13 continues from the third and fourth academic years:

Fourteen, Consume a balanced diet with adequate nutrients at each meal.

Fifteen, Maintain a proper distance between the eyes and the object when reading and writing (between 30 and 40 centimeters).

Sixteen, Sleep at 8 PM every night and wake up at 6 AM the next morning. Get out of bed immediately after waking up in the morning.

Seventeen, Fold and arrange your bedding neatly every day after getting out of bed.

Eighteen, Maintain overall neatness and appearance. Prevent spraying saliva when talking to others.

Knowledge and Skills Personal The study and practice of the following items 1 to 9 continue from the third and fourth academic years:

Ten, The functions and health care of the circulatory, excretory, and nervous systems.

Eleven, Essential nutrients (water, air, sunlight, vitamins, proteins, fats, starches, organic salts), developmental factors (food, sleep, air, sunlight, exercise, rest).

Twelve, The absorption and digestion of nutrients; the causes of nearsightedness and farsightedness; the harms of alcohol, tobacco, and other stimulating foods; methods of rest; the benefits of exercise; methods of regulating temperature; caution with cold and raw foods.

Thirteen, The relationship between diseases and medicines (not all diseases necessarily require medication); the relationship between patients and those who treat them (patients should follow the guidance of those who treat them); the selection of doctors.

Fourteen, Prevention of infectious diseases and their vectors.

Fifteen, First aid essentials (controlling bleeding, drowning, burns, bone fractures, joint dislocations, artificial respiration, methods of transporting patients, bandaging).

Sixteen, Anecdotes from medical history.

Public The study and practice of the following items 1 to 12 continue from the third and fourth academic years:

Thirteen, Study environmental relationships (proper disposal of feces, establishment of tap water systems, installation of sewers, rat extermination, silkworm eradication, etc.).

Fourteen, Safeguarding public safety (safety and disaster drills in residential, travel, transportation, and entertainment venues).

Fifteen, Improving the living environment (overseeing the improvement of public health initiatives in the home and community environment, and participating in various health campaigns).

Sixteen, Promoting community health (promoting public health initiatives, instilling personal hygiene knowledge, organizational methods for health cooperatives, etc.).

Seventeen, Understanding the importance of hygiene facilities, mortality surveys, infectious disease surveys, birth surveys, and the significance of conducting other health initiatives.

Eighteen, Participating in public health initiatives (visits to local health administrative agencies, water plants, sewers, medical schools, etc.; designing health initiatives within the school and surrounding areas; practicing various health services).

Nineteen, Infant care knowledge (applicable to female students).

Weekly time: 60 minutes

Fourth, Teaching Key Points

1. Hygiene education should start with practical problems; practice is more important than knowledge. 2. Teachers should strive to integrate hygiene knowledge with the practical environment during teaching, fully adopt the spirit of project-based teaching, and increase connections with other subjects and extracurricular activities for children. 3. Teachers should lead by example during teaching and personally participate in practical work related to hygiene. 4. Teachers must actively inspect children's hygiene practices, regularly examine various hygiene habits and skills, and conduct daily cleanliness checks for children in lower grades at any time. Various assessments and inspections should be recorded with symbols or scores, and the results should be statistically analyzed to promote interest in practice through competition. 5. Schools should, within their means, fully provide various equipment related to hygiene to enable children to use them at any time and create a hygienic environment. 6. Schools should, within their means, designate a room as the office for all school hygiene facilities. 7. Schools should, within their means, invite local health officials or parents enthusiastic about hygiene education to form a school health education design committee to lead the promotion of health education. 8. Schools should, within their means, independently or jointly with nearby schools, hire doctors and nurses to oversee school health matters. 9. Various hygiene groups, such as cleanliness inspection teams, nursing teams, and small hospitals, should be organized within children's activity groups for practice. 10. Implementing hygiene education requires full communication with families for effective results; otherwise, there will be many difficulties in progress. Therefore, during home visits or parent-teacher conferences, information about hygiene facilities should be discussed, or parents should be guided to visit children's hygiene self-governance organizations and school hygiene equipment. 11. In addition to daily hygiene inspections and monthly height and weight measurements, a general hygiene inspection or hygiene competition must be held regularly each academic year, and the results should be distributed and reported to families. 12. A hygiene education assessment must be conducted at the end of each semester to examine the progress of school hygiene education for comparison and improvement. 13. Children must be fully involved in various social hygiene gatherings in the community, such as cleaning and fly-swatting teams. 14. Children must practically investigate or visit various public health and public safety facilities or organizations in the community to cultivate their interest in public health and public safety.

Central Aviation School to Recruit Students in Peiping

▲Yesterday, a Telegram Was Sent to Jiang Menglin to Borrow an Examination Site

The Central Aviation School, to cultivate Chinese aviation talent, has added advanced refresher courses in military and mechanical engineering, and will gradually recall existing aviation personnel for advanced training. It is learned that the school has scheduled to continue recruiting new students in January next year, with recruitment examinations to be held in major cities across the country. In Peiping, it has been decided to send personnel to oversee everything by the end of this year, with the examination period set from January 1st to 3rd next year. The school's President, Ge Jing'en, sent a telegram to Jiang Menglin, President of Peiping University, to borrow an examination site that can accommodate a large number of people, and to borrow several rooms that can handle registration and physical examinations from December 22nd of this year, to be used as examination office locations. If Peiping University has any inconveniences, please contact Peking University or Normal University to arrange for personnel to go and make arrangements as soon as possible.

Local News

Executive Committee Meeting of the French Concession Private School Federation

▲Starting Today, Broadcasting Lectures on Radio Stations

▲Chinese Director Wei Tingrong Sent a Letter Yesterday to Arrange a Meeting Today

▲The Municipal Education Association Sent a Letter Requesting Chinese Directors to Strive Together

The Federation of Private Primary and Secondary Schools in the French Concession of this city is actively making every effort to request funding from the French Municipal Council. Yesterday, it convened the third executive committee meeting to discuss several important cases. Yesterday, Chinese Director Wei Tingrong scheduled a meeting for today due to important matters. The Municipal Education Association sent a letter to all Chinese Directors urging them to strive together. The details are as follows:

▲Executive Committee Meeting Attendees: Executive Committee members Hua Dong Ma Jiazhen, Minzhong Hong Guang, Nanshang Mao Zhaorong, Chongshi Shen Xibin, Lehua Song An; Observers An Xu of the Supervisory Committee, Mao Dexu, Dehua Wang Dingcheng, Tianhua Gong Yuyi, and others. Chairman: Hong Guang. Key cases decided: 1. Send a letter to the Chinese Taxpayers Association and Chinese Directors to strive for the implementation of subsidies for private schools starting in 1933. 2. Send a letter to the preparatory committee of the Municipal Residents Association to unanimously advocate for assistance. 3. Each school in the federation will send one representative to the French Municipal Council next Monday at 9:00 AM to petition, and gather at Minsheng Primary School beforehand. 4. Appoint standing committee members to request assistance from the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Education Bureau. 5. All executive and supervisory committee members will take turns broadcasting and lecturing in Mandarin, English, and French on various radio stations every day to awaken the attention of the citizens. 6. Approve Shangcai, Wenchang, Jianzhong, Huaxin, and four other schools as members of the federation (the rest omitted). Meeting adjourned.

▲Today's Petition In addition to petitioning Chinese Committee Member Cheng Zhusun and Chinese Director Zhu Yan to strive for the cause, yesterday the association originally intended to visit Chinese Directors Wei Tingrong and Lu Bohong. However, Mr. Wei sent a letter stating that he had other matters that day and arranged to meet today at 9:30 AM. After receiving the letter, the association decided that standing committee members Ma Jiazhen, Hong Guang, and Mao Zhaorong will represent the association for the visit this morning.

▲Letter from the Education Association Yesterday, the Municipal Education Association sent a letter to the Chinese Directors of the French Municipal Council to assist the federation, stating: "Respected Sirs, we have received a letter from the Federation of Private Primary and Secondary Schools in the French Concession stating (original letter omitted) that the revenue budget of the French Municipal Council for the whole year shows that Chinese taxpayers contribute more than two-thirds of the tax revenue, while the educational funding received by the Chinese is only about one percent. Comparing this to the number of Western children and the allocation of educational funding within the Concession, the Municipal Council should allocate 20% of the annual revenue to expand Chinese educational funding. This is merely a demand based on a comparative limit and a right that Chinese in the Concession should have. Our association deeply sympathizes with this proposal. We have prepared this letter accordingly, and we hope that you gentlemen will argue with the French Concession authorities based on reason and strive to achieve the above-mentioned objectives, so as to expand Chinese education within the Concession and enhance public relations."

Declaration by the Education Association of the Second District of This City Demanding the Development of Chinese Education

The Education Association of the Second District of this city believes that the French Concession authorities do not pay enough attention to Chinese education and that Western children receive far better treatment. Therefore, a declaration was issued, requesting Chinese Directors to suggest to the French Municipal Council that Chinese and Western children receive equal treatment. The original text is recorded below: "Since Shanghai opened as a port and the French established a concession, the disparity between Chinese and Western taxpayers has been significant. Chinese taxpayers contribute more than two-thirds of the revenue, but the treatment they receive is far less than that of Westerners, especially in the field of education within the Concession. Comparing the annual per capita educational expenditure of Western and Chinese children within the Concession will immediately reveal the disparity in treatment by the French Municipal Council. According to recent statistics from the French Municipal Council, there are a total of 125,700 Chinese children within the Concession, while the annual educational expenditure is only 88,200 taels. The per capita educational expenditure for Chinese children is only 7 jiao and 1 fen. There are only 2,737 Western children within the Concession, but the annual educational expenditure is as high as 130,000 taels. The per capita educational expenditure for Western children is 44 taels. Based on the above statistics, the French Municipal Council's neglect of Chinese education is evident. To develop Chinese education within the Concession, we must urge the French Municipal Council to reflect and improve or promote Chinese schools, or subsidize private schools within the Concession. At the same time, we should request Chinese Directors to make every effort to suggest to the French Municipal Council that Chinese and Western children receive equal treatment. Only then will the relationship between China and France be harmonious. We hereby declare."

Talking About Xingzhong's Return Home After Completing His Studies

Mr. Tan Xingzhong, a native of Yixing, graduated from Tongde Medical University in his eighteenth year. Because he felt that his knowledge was not enough to serve the world, he went to Germany to specialize in medicine. He usually studied tuberculosis, and he was particularly skilled in artificial pneumothorax and phrenic nerve resection. He had profound knowledge and rich experience. After spending three years in Germany, he obtained a doctorate this spring. Afterwards, he traveled to famous hospitals in Austria and Switzerland. He returned to China on an Italian mail ship in the middle of last month and has now arrived in Shanghai. Many people from the medical and academic communities have contacted him recently.

Patriotic Girls' School to Hold 31st Anniversary Celebration

The Patriotic Girls' School on Jiangwan Road in this city has a history of 31 years. The curriculum is usually very serious, and the school affairs are developing day by day. Although this academic year has been affected by the war, the school has gradually restored its old appearance with the efforts and planning of the new principal, Sun Xiangzhong. In addition to the senior and junior high school and sports courses, a female scout trainer training class has been specially established to create specialized female trainers. The school's participation in the Jiangsu Provincial Jamboree was highly praised by the central committee members. In order to connect feelings, the school will hold a 31st anniversary celebration on the second day of next month (Friday) and perform various entertainment and new dramas.

National Primary School Holds a Carnival

Although National Primary School in Kangle Lane, Xinzha Road, has only been established for one year, its achievements are remarkable. Recently, due to the expansion of school buildings and the increase in students, the funding has become tight. Principal Xu Huimin discussed with the school board to initiate a fundraising carnival. The entertainment programs that have been successfully contacted include Beijing opera by Shanghai amateur actors Wang Detian and Yuan Ludeng, and colleagues from the Postal Workers' Union, spoken drama, singing and dancing by Shanghai Girls' High School, celebrity comedy, and martial arts performances by Qiu Yan, etc. It is reported that the location has been tentatively set at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and is approved to open next Sunday, with both day and night performances.

Xu Qingyu's Collection of Speeches to be Published Soon

Xu Qingyu, the Standing Committee Member of the World Society and the current Director of the Jiangxi County Training Institute, often goes to various places to give speeches after returning from studying at Oxford University. His speeches have been edited into a book by Yang Daying and printed in Nanchang. It can be published soon. The content is divided into four major issues: culture, politics, philosophy, and youth. 1. Cultural issues include four articles: Mechanical Industry and Culture, Chinese Nationalities and World Culture, Stoddard's Theory of Culture, and Filial Piety and Chinese Culture. 2. Political issues include five articles: The Position of the Three Principles of the People in Modern Political Thought, the Ironclad Evidence of Capitalism Manufacturing Imperialism, China of Tomorrow, the Psychology of National Extinction and National Salvation, and the Establishment of a Leader's Nation. 3. Philosophical issues include seven articles: My Seven Beliefs, the Position of Confucius' Philosophy Today, the New Philosophy of Life, the Evolution of the Heart, Confucius and Mr. Sun Yat-sen, the New Egoism, and Philosophy and National Salvation. 4. Youth issues include six articles: The Way Out for Youth, the Philosophy of Life That Young Women Should Have, High School Students and Chinese Language, Youth Cultivation and National Revolution, Love and the Development of Youth Personality, Youth's Worries and Their Remedies are all representative works of Xu. The book price is six cents and will be sold by Kaiming Bookstore and the Youth Association Bookstore.

Establishment of the Huang Ke Gymnasium

In recent years, China's sports development has advanced by leaps and bounds. This is indeed a good sign for the future of Chinese sports. The Kearney Physical Education School at 11 Seymour Road, founded by Kearney, has a history of over ten years since the Republic year 10. However, Chinese individuals aspiring to engage in sports have had no means to do so. Currently, Dr. Huang Miao, the principal of Zhengfeng Middle School, recognizing this, consulted with Kearney and obtained his consent to convert the Kearney Physical Education School into a Chinese-run institution, renamed the Huang Ke Gymnasium, with Huang serving as the director. Kearney will serve as the director of the Western sports department.

Xia Guang Basketball Team Suffers a Narrow Defeat Last Night

▲ Lost to McLain by Two Points in the Last Minute

▲ Final Score: 33 to 31

John Wins Over Nan Xing

No Games Tonight

Last night in the Western Youth Basketball League, Xia Guang suffered a narrow defeat to McLain by two points in the last minute. The final score was 33 to 31. The tension in the air was unprecedented since the beginning of the season. In another match, John defeated Nan Xing 37 to 32, which was less exciting. Tonight there will be women's basketball games, and the men will have a day of rest.

▲ Xia Guang's Loss Was a Pity

▲ Xia Guang's Momentum

Xia Guang came onto the court with great momentum, leading 4-2 and then 8-2. Chen Baoqiu's successful free throw made it 9-2, giving them a significant advantage and creating the impression that they would sweep McLain. However, in an instant, due to slightly lax defense, McLain seized the opportunity to counterattack with successive advances. McLain scored 11 points, taking the lead at 13-9. McLain then won the first half with a score of 15-11.

▲ Ups and Downs

Xia Guang, initially with the advantage, was chased by McLain. The offense and defense became more rigorous than before, and the match became closer and more intense. Despite the efforts of Ren and Wei, they only managed to catch up to 16-15. They then made it 18-17, taking a one-point lead. However, McLain responded with 19-18 and 21-20, regaining a one-point lead. The ebb and flow were endless, making it difficult to predict, and the excitement increased accordingly.

▲ Exciting Finale

Xia Guang was only one point behind, but then Monaghan scored consecutively, and McLain extended their lead to 27-22, creating a five-point gap. This sparked a thrilling comeback. Guan Dang'an's long-range shot and Ren Jiexing's success allowed Xia Guang to display excellent teamwork, tying the score again at 27-27. As the end of the game approached, the atmosphere became extremely tense.

▲ Final Crushing Defeat

After 27-27, McLain regained the lead with 29-27 and then 31-29, each time leading by only two points. Chen Baoqiu then made a sudden basket, tying the score again at 31-31. However, in the final tens of seconds, Byeshpol's shot led to Xia Guang's crushing defeat.

▲ Reasons for the Setback

Xia Guang had more opportunities than McLain last night, and McLain missed many inaccurate shots. Xia Guang had a great chance of winning, but their fatal flaw was their stagnation after taking a 9-2 lead in the first half, with lax defense and slow movements, allowing McLain to overtake them and score over ten points consecutively. Although they tried hard in the second half, it was too late. Chen Baoqiu's subpar performance was also a reason for their failure to win.

The Surprisingly Good Qunqun Volleyball Team

▲ Today at 4 PM: Maiden Match Against Soochow University

Guangdong volleyball has always been the best in the country, and almost all representatives to the Far Eastern Games in the past have been from Guangdong. Therefore, it is no exaggeration to say that Guangdong is the origin of volleyball. Now, the Qunqun Society students from Peizheng Middle School in Guangzhou, who have recently arrived in Shanghai, deeply feel that volleyball in Shanghai is inactive. In order to promote this sport, they have organized a volleyball team with their friends in Shanghai to play friendly matches with various military and business groups. The team members include prominent players from Soochow University and Fudan University, such as Mo Jinliu, Wang Jiajun, Li Bifu, Huang Shaojie, Zhou Jieming, and Chen Bocai, all of whom are skilled in this sport. Today is their maiden match against Soochow University. The location is the Soochow University volleyball court in Yangshupu. Fans, don't miss this opportunity.

News from the First Municipal Industrial and Commercial Football Association

The fourth industrial and commercial amateur football competition at the First Municipal Sports Field will allow teams with at least eleven players who participated last year to register, preserving the qualifications of veteran members to continue competing, as previously reported. It is now learned that the registration for the association has closed. The list of teams that have applied to continue as veteran members includes the Postal Workers, Baohua, Central, Puyi, Qiuxin, Jianguang, Zuzhu, Xin Xin, Mian Guang, Northeast, Hui Guang, Lianyi, Hua Zhan, Pu Song, Chen Guang, Qiang Nan, Asia, Xin Yi Shao Guang, Shi Gong, Ling Nan, Gao Qiao, Meiya, Xin Xin, Guanghu, Zhi Yong, You Ning, Zhi Hua, and Dong Hua, Yang Zhi teams. However, after verifying the registration lists from last year, it was found that the Guanghu, Zhi Yong, You Ning, Zhi Hua, Dong Hua, and Yang Zhi teams did not have at least eleven veteran members, rendering their applications invalid according to regulations. Other teams, such as Xudong, Hongmao, Hunan, Huzhi, Shi Tu, Ye Shi, and Qingyun, with fewer veteran members than required, have strongly requested to continue participating. The association has granted them permission to re-register and join the competition from today until the 31st of November. Late registrations will not be accepted. Also, if the communication address of a registered team has changed, it must be notified in writing before the 31st.

New Basketball Techniques (3)(4) (Not to be Reprinted) Original by Mlaire Burcky, Translated by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin

Russell (Pug) Daughyity, former star of the Enos football and basketball teams, and now the basketball coach at Rice Institution, often uses this strategy to surprise and win after the jump ball, when the opponent's lineup is not yet complete. However, it must be noted that the center of our team must be able to jump over the opponent's center for this strategy to be effective.

Center #3 taps the ball to #4, who crosses the court behind the opponent's center. At this time, #4 should not hesitate and immediately pass the ball back to #3, who has retreated from the center circle. At the same time, #2 quickly sprints down from the right sideline. #3 immediately passes the ball long to #2. #1 also crosses the court to the basket to anticipate the pass from #2, or to rebound and put the ball in if #2 misses the shot.

Free Talk

One or Two Random Thoughts

My Baldness

— Zhan Lu

There are different types of hair: sandy hair and cottony hair. Sandy hair is close to hardening, while cottony hair is close to softening. In youth, there are no significant differences between sandy hair and cottony hair. But after middle age, sandy hair is more likely to turn white but less likely to become bald, while cottony hair is more likely to become bald but less likely to turn white. This is a marvel of nature, "compensating the essence with fat," "one mantis shrimp matches one shrimp," ensuring that neither suffers a loss and each has its advantages and disadvantages. I belong to the cottony hair type. I only just reached middle age, and the frontline of my hair has been unable to maintain its original state, with some lines wavering. Now, needless to say, lines of defense are retreating one by one, already retreating to the third line of defense! However, even though the lines of defense are retreating, no white flag has been raised. This is a characteristic of cottony hair and something to be proud of.

Patting my head, although not completely bald, the character "xiu" (秀, elegant) in "xiucai" (秀才, scholar), with its curved tail, cannot escape the character for baldness ("tu" 秃). Speaking plainly about baldness, let me tell two bald stories for amusement:

Ji Zisun, a senior official of the state of Lu in the Spring and Autumn period, was bald. He, along with Qu Ke, a lame official of the state of Jin, Gongzi Shou, a hunchbacked prince of the state of Cao, and Sun Liangfu, a one-eyed minister of the state of Wei, were all sent to Qi as envoys. The Duke of Qi also chose bald, lame, hunchbacked, and one-eyed people to serve as their drivers, which greatly angered the guests, leading to a fierce battle. I believe that lameness, hunchback, and blindness are disabilities. It is understandable that the envoys of Jin, Cao, and Wei were angry. Baldness is a stage that older people inevitably go through. Ji Zisun's anger is truly unjustifiable.

If it were a foreign bald person, they would wish to have other bald people as their companions. The recent bald convention has already become a popular tale. Let's set that aside for now. In the past, there was a Duke in Bulgaria who, after losing his hair due to illness and becoming bald, had over five hundred nobles shave their heads, revealing their shiny tops, to become his bald comrades. The Duke happily associated with them, pleased that he was not alone in his baldness. This Duke's tolerance was different from Ji Zisun of Lu. Ji Zisun was already angered by a bald driver. If these five hundred bald men had surrounded him, his bald head would probably have burst into flames! Haha!

China Through American Eyes

— Xu Bo'an

丨China Is No Worse Than America丨

I once heard Mr. Muegen, an American professor at Zhijiang University, say these words. "You shouldn't think that China is already beyond repair and idealize our American nation and society as excellent and perfect. This prejudice is probably influenced by Dr. Hu Shih's propaganda. Based on my observations, I don't think China is any worse than America. For example, private opium trafficking is rampant in China, but American private alcohol smuggling is comparable. For example, there are many kidnapping cases in Shanghai, sometimes as many as five or six a day, but in bustling American cities like New York and Chicago, there are sometimes over seventy cases in one night! And wasn't aviator Lindbergh's son kidnapped last semester? In fact, the increase in crime and the progress of civilization are racing forward at the same rate. American material civilization is higher than China's, so the degree of crime is also higher than China's, that is without a doubt. The only difference is that American capitalists and their kept politicians are better at organizing and using their skills to cover up many ugly things in the lowest layers of society, while painting a dazzling layer of gold on the upper layers. Thus, shallow-minded people praise the gold, forgetting the evil beneath it. In contrast, the situation in China is different. The upper layers are ugly, but the lower layers are no more ugly than that. Indeed,"

Big Dishes and Flatbread

— Wan Cheng

Eating big dishes represents the aristocratic class, and eating flatbread represents the poor class. Why do both "big dishes" and "flatbread" use the character "big" (大)? It actually contains philosophical meaning.

Our theory is that eating big dishes is definitely happier than eating flatbread!

In fact, let's look at rickshaw pullers, after toiling like animals, when their stomachs are rumbling and they desperately need food, holding a flatbread and chewing it. They seem to feel immense pleasure in their nerves, and their stomachs urgently need it. Although they are eating flatbread, its flavor is endless! It surpasses the taste of the big dishes eaten by aristocrats!

Conversely, think about the delicacies and banquets that aristocrats eat every day. But they are probably not as flavorful as the flatbread eaten by the poor.

Therefore, "flatbread" is also called "big." Although the item is cheap, the poor get it and are also "greatly" pleased with their meal. All worldly matters should be viewed in this way.

The Chinese and Gambling

— Qingke

From childhood, when they bought candy with a few copper coins, they were already infected with gambling and received gambling training. Entertainment and games, of all kinds, contain elements of gambling to some extent and are inseparable from gambling.

As for gambling with money, gambling with wives, and gambling with lives, that is simply competing to win or lose, it is a dog-eat-dog struggle. "Life is originally a gamble." Chinese people have such a passionate "fighting" view of life, which is remarkable.

Life should be about getting rich. And getting rich depends 70% on luck and 30% on effort. Chinese people are most superstitious about fatalism, which can be seen in gambling. But gambling itself is just blind luck, an accidental opportunity, so their philosophy is a completely muddled and random view of history. It's best to win at gambling, but it's okay to lose a little. They understand that "neither winning nor losing" is boring, neither good nor bad, what's the point? How do you explain luck?

Therefore, gambling needs a bit of boldness. But gambling also needs a lot of greed and a chance mentality. Chinese people are easily enticed by profit. It also needs small cleverness, cunning, deception, etc. Also, it needs a risk-taking attitude. We know that the "gambling spirit" of Guangdong people and other "Southern Barbarians" is famous. They are quick-witted, decisive, and have a genius for risk-taking. Even the signs of restaurants are written with terms like "zhong fa bai," "qing yi se," "da san yuan," and other such words. You can guess that their mahjong skills must be top-notch. Just imagine, at the moment of the so-called "all-in," what courage and spirit! How many of the shy, cowardly, and not-so-bold Jiangnan people have this?

Crossroads of Death (22)

— Fan Yanqiao

"Alas, this won't work. The older generation in their families doesn't want to join the army. If you tell them, they definitely won't agree. It's best to make up your own mind. I mean well because I heard you say that life is tough, and you can't make a name for yourself your whole life. It's not bad to go out and see the green mountains and clear waters, make more friends, and gain more knowledge. It's up to you whether you go or not. I can't push you too much, or you'll blame me in the future."

"How many days will you be delayed?"

Jiang Niupi counted on his fingers, looking up and saying, "Today is the 21st, not counting, the 22nd to Suzhou to see friends, the 23rd back, the 24th to Dongshan to entrust a few acres of barren land to someone, the 25th maybe delayed there, the 26th back, the 27th will set off, still in time to go to Jiujiang to collect pay at the end of the month."

"There are five whole days, enough for me to think about it."

Jiang Niupi picked off the remaining cigarette butt that was burning the bamboo pipe, blew on it, put it in his pocket, drank a cup of tea in one gulp, and stood up, saying,

"Think it over, then give me an answer."

A'gen also stood up and said insincerely, "Come to my house for a meal before you leave."

"No need to be polite, I have a relative waiting for me. See you later!" He unintentionally stretched his right hand to his right temple, giving an incomplete salute.

A'gen also secretly laughed.

By the evening of the 26th, A'gen's restlessness was indescribable. Liu Da sat on a stone slab under the pumpkin trellis, smoking a dry pipe. Liu's wife sat on a stool made of a tree stump, peeling sunflower seeds. The setting sun shone through the half-yellow pumpkin vines, shining on the faces of the two old people, making them look even more yellow, like two dusty, peeling statues of the Earth God and Earth Goddess, haphazardly placed beside the "Ingredient Division" counter. Only A'gen's face was filled with blood and his spirit was invigorated, like a Spartan warrior from a Western print. One moment, he was depressed, lowering his head and kicking the small bricks on the mud floor, wishing he could kick away everything in the world that hindered life's progress. He wanted to say something, but there was a Master who wouldn't allow it. The things he wasn't allowed to say were stuck in his throat, even worse than having "catarrh" in his throat. Suddenly, Liu's wife broke the lonely evening scene by saying,

"This pumpkin is really big, at least ten pounds. We don't need to cook tomorrow night, let's eat pumpkin."

A'gen heard this and was again touched. If he left with Jiang tomorrow, he wouldn't get to eat this big pumpkin.

Grain Market Situation at Hexia Continues to Weaken]

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, sources from various groups were still arriving in a continuous stream, numbering about fifty. The amount stored in the docks was not substantial. Shops in the city and countryside were connected at the end, and as the sluice gate market was generally weak, people felt indifferent and transactions decreased sharply compared to before. The price of thick japonica rice suddenly dropped slightly. Arrivals of late-season rice were not weak, but transactions on this street remained thin. Transactions of Ningbo glutinous rice were also fragmented, and the market price was slightly reduced. The price of foreign Dujian rice fluctuated.

(Xinzha) There were thirty to forty sources on the west road, and there were some transactions on this street. Changzhou and Wuxi japonica rice with added foot was the most traded, and the price was stable. The rice market in Suzhou and Kunshan was quiet, and prices were weak by one or two cents. Sales of early and late-season rice were slow, and the market followed suit. Quanzhou merchants actively handled customer indica rice.

Yesterday, the foreign customer indica rice market was initially weak, but then local customers made inquiries, and the market began to stabilize. Quanzhou merchants suddenly showed strong interest, and Fuzhou merchants also actively handled shipments, turning the market from weak to active. On this street, another Saigon shipment of 400 bags was sold. The foreign rice market also became firm. However, customer indica rice arrived continuously at the port, and yesterday, two more ships of Hunan and Jiangxi rice arrived. Currently, the market has ample supply. Although Fujian province is buying, supply exceeds demand, and the market will likely find it difficult to expand. Although customer sales were active yesterday, the price was slightly lower by a fraction. The overall market quoted Saigon No. 1 rice at 400 bags, with the price remaining at 8 yuan. Jiangxi machine-milled late rice at 761 bags was priced at 8 yuan, 57 cents to 8 yuan and 50 cents, and another 50 bags of machine-milled yuan rice were priced at 11 yuan. Hunan machine-milled oil rice at 507 bags was priced at 8 yuan, 82 cents to 8 yuan and 78 cents. Saigon rice was purchased by merchants from this street, machine-milled yuan rice by merchants from Fuzhou, and the rest by merchants from Quanzhou.

Flour Market: Near Weak, Far Firm

Yesterday, the flour market saw sluggish spot sales, with no further purchasing as previous purchases had been too large, and appetites were satisfied. For the time being, people are watching and waiting, hoping to take action again after the market price weakens. This month, due to spot goods, prices are also softening. However, forward contracts are being supported by mill positions, and the market is recovering from weakness. After the market opened in the morning, the price of foreign wheat was reported to be slightly lower, and people became cautious. However, mills were not dumping their positions, and it was difficult to lower prices further. Therefore, trading was slow and the market was stable. In the afternoon, the market became more active. At the close, November was down .025, December was up .075, January to March were all up .075, and April was up .025.

Wheat Market: Trend Remains Stable

Yesterday, the wheat market was sluggish in both the morning and afternoon sessions, with few transactions. Prices were slightly lower as the price of foreign wheat fell by about 2 cents, and there was Australian wheat selling for 3.5 taels. People in the market were generally cautious, and forward contracts were especially weak. In the afternoon, the price of Australian wheat rose, and it was difficult to secure orders. As the flour market turned around, those shorting the market did not continue to sell, and those with open positions were looking to cover. However, sales were very limited, and trading was even more subdued. At the close, the current month was up .01, and there were no comparable prices for December, January, and February. April was also up .01.

Chicago Wheat Continues to Weaken

A report from the New Feng Foreign Firm stated that on Monday (the 21st), Chicago wheat fell across all periods due to poor foreign demand and long positions being liquidated. On the 19th, a total of 20 million bushels were traded. The market prices for the 21st are listed below:

Dried Goods and Nut Stall Guild Decides to Reduce Prices

The supply of dried longan has been increasing recently, while sales have been decreasing. Although there are restrictions on sales prices set by the guild, competition has intensified due to fewer buyers, leading to hidden discounts and a chaotic pricing situation. To rectify this, the guild convened a meeting yesterday and decided to uniformly reduce prices for all grades of dried longan to standardize them. The top grade is set at 33 taels, Tianji at 17 taels, Tianhong at 13 taels, peeled at 9 taels, Zheng Er at 8.5 taels, and Pao Yuan at 8 taels (local and inland areas to be added).

Sugar Market: Actual Sales of Sugar Goods Increase

The sugar market saw little change in the standard price, but sales suddenly surged, raising expectations and causing prices to rise. The guild's standard price for No. 24 coarse granulated white ordinary sugar was initially set at 15 taels, 9 qian, 2 fen, 5 li, but later rose to 9 qian, 5 fen, an increase of 5 to 7.5 fen from the previous day, with about 3,000 bags traded. High-quality goods were priced at 15 taels and 0.05 fen. No. 18 and No. 20 medium granulated white sugar were stable. No. 8 Hechi new goods were 11 taels and 6 qian, up 5 fen; old goods were 11 taels and 2 qian, up a qian. No. 9 old Hechi was 11 taels and 5.5 qian, No. 10 old goods were 11 taels, 6 qian, 2 fen, 5 li, and high No. 11 was 12 taels. Taikoo car sugar BCWDY brands all remained at the original price, and HX brand was 15 taels, 1 qian, 5 fen, up 5 fen. Chaozhou merchants offered Huizhou sugar excluding 60-70 bags at a price of 11 taels and 8 qian. Small brick sugar was reported to have arrived continuously, and the goods were very dry and light in color.

Silk and Tea Foreign Firms: Silk Market Weakens Further

Yesterday, the local foreign firms' silk market continued to be weak and quiet. Telegrams regarding American silk prices remained unchanged. European firms, seeing the sluggishness of overseas silk prices, considered lowering prices and stockpiling. Chinese silk merchants were unwilling to sell at a loss, leading to a sluggish market. Exports of Douppion silk were increasingly rare.

Exports of Douppion silk to Europe have remained stagnant for a long time, and overseas silk prices have plummeted. In Shanghai, only Fulun Silk Factory is still operating. Recently, sales to France have remained sluggish, and sales of Douppion silk have been sluggish. On this French postal ship "Qin Liao Mei Jing", only 15 bales of Douppion silk were exported to Marseille.

Zhejiang's Old Mill Silk is Continuously Shipped to Shanghai

A total of over 700 bales

Since receiving three announcements from the Committee for Sorting Old Silkworm Cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, silk and cocoon merchants in Jiangsu and Zhejiang have respectively reported and registered the quantity of old mill silk and dried cocoons in their possession so that they can enjoy duty-free and 100 tael subsidy per bale when old mill silk is exported. It is learned that the issuance of Jiangsu-Zhejiang silk industry public bonds is imminent. Silk and cocoon merchants in Hangzhou, Shaoxing, and Huzhou, Zhejiang, who hold old cocoons, are actively entrusting local silk mills to produce silk, transport it to Shanghai for storage. Therefore, the shipping of old mill silk to Shanghai is not weak, with a total of 778 bales being shipped.

Needle and Eyebrow Green Tea Sells Well in Europe

Yesterday, Yingzhuang, Qiahe, Xiehe, Jinlong, and Tongfu firms showed strong interest in needle and eyebrow green tea from Wuyuan and Tunxi. However, due to thin inventories, supply could not meet demand. Most merchants were searching for Gongxi tea to be processed into needle and eyebrow tea. As for Zhenmei green tea, there were still over 20,000 boxes in inventory. Although Yingzhuang firms had some sales yesterday, the prices offered were too low, and Chinese tea merchants could not agree to the deals due to large losses. Transactions for other Gongxi goods were also declining.

Hardware: English Steel Plate Scarce and Expensive

Hardware transactions have been peaceful recently. Due to tight credit, foreign merchants are not as eager to make large purchases as before. Manufacturers, except for purchasing essential goods, are less inclined to stockpile. Fortunately, imports of various goods are not large, so there have not been significant changes in prices. However, some popular items have limited arrivals, so the standard price is rising. For example, English steel plates have been purchased by various merchants recently, leading to a shortage of inventory and soaring prices. 2% can be estimated at 8 taels 2 qian 5 fen, 5% at 6 taels 2 qian 5 fen, 7% at 6 taels, 10% at 5 taels 9 qian, and above 15% is estimated at 5 taels 7 qian 5 fen. However, overseas arrivals are rare, so prices are expected to rise further. Other items such as bamboo joint steel bars, new silver dollars, white tile, and tinplate are also showing signs of continued increases. Judging from the current hardware market, falling prices are as rare as phoenix feathers and unicorn horns.
