Local News Two First Special Court Opened Yesterday Anhui Northern Relief Wheat Scandal Only First Defendant Yang Shucheng Was Interrogated Then It Stopped Zha Liangzhao Debated and Counter-Sued, With Incidental Civil Suit Requesting Compensation for 500,000 Half for Relief, Half for School ### The Shocking Anhui Northern Relief Wheat Scandal: After the Shanghai Fellow-Provincials Association Filed a Private Prosecution with the First Special District Court Against Yang Shucheng, Quan Shaowu, Wang Fanwu, Zha Liangzhao, and Others, Staff of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, It Has Been Heard Twice. As the Four Defendants Were All Outside the City, They Were Unable to Attend Court. Yesterday Afternoon at 2 PM, the Trial Was Held in the Criminal Court Two of the First Special District Court. The Original Defendants and Defense Lawyers, Including Zhang Shizhao, Were All Present. On the Plaintiff's Side, Li Zhenya Spoke. The Defendants Yang Shucheng, Quan Shaowu, Wang Fanwu, Zha Liangzhao, and Others Stood in the Defendant's Column. After the Judge Asked Their Names, Ages, Native Places, and Occupations, Zha Liangzhao, Due to Illness, Was Ordered to Sit in the Witness Stand. The Debate Began Regarding Yang Shucheng's Abuse of Power, Obstructing Transportation, Purchasing Relief Wheat, and Selling It at a High Price. The American Baker, Head of the Transportation Department of the Disaster Relief Association, Was Immediately Called to Testify. The Court Adjourned at Half Past Four, Ordering a Continued Hearing on the Afternoon of the 25th. Zha Liangzhao Hired Lawyers Such as Zhang Shizhao to Draft a Defense and File a Counter-Suit. The Debate and Zha's Statement Are Recorded Below. ▲Debate: First, Li Zhenya, Representative of the Anhui Fellow-Provincials Association, Stated That Last Year, the 21 Counties in Northern Anhui Suffered a Major Flood. Some of the Relief Workers Delayed Transportation and Purchased Relief Wheat to Sell at a High Price for Personal Gain. The Shanghai Fellow-Provincials Association Received Repeated Appeals and Reports From Representatives of the Disaster Victims in Northern Anhui. They Did Not Dare to Believe Such Heartless Behavior. Later, They Sent Two Commissioners Each With the Beijing Fellow-Provincials Association Relief Committee to Northern Anhui to Conduct a Factual Investigation and Obtained 100 Pieces of Evidence. After the Association Received the Investigators' Report, They Believed That the Disaster Relief Committee Would Take Appropriate Measures to Resolve the Situation. Unexpectedly, After a Long Time, There Was Still No Response, So They Had No Choice but to Seek a Legal Solution. Later, the Plaintiff's Lawyer, Li Shirui, Stated That the First Defendant, Yang Shucheng, 1. Used His Power to Stop the Transportation of Relief Wheat in Order to Transport His Own Purchased Wheat. From January 18th to February 10th, Not a Single Grain of Relief Wheat Was Transported From Pukou to Bengbu. During This Cold Winter, How Many Disaster Victims Starved to Death? 2. Transported His Privately Purchased Wheat, Pretending It Was Relief Wheat, Free of Charge. 3. Claimed That It Was Difficult to Transport Relief Wheat, So He Sold 10,000 Tons to the Baoxing Flour Mill, Which Yang Solely Owned. Most of It Was Delivered in Bengbu. If It Was Necessary to Sell Because Relief Wheat Could Not Be Transported to Bengbu, and It Was Already in Bengbu, Then Why Sell It? 4. The Relief Wheat That Yang Purchased Cost Over 80 Yuan Per Ton, While the Price of Wheat in Bengbu Was 7 to 10 Yuan Per Stone, Which Is Over 120 to 170 Yuan Per Ton. With a Single Transfer, He Would Profit at Least 40 Yuan. Yang Purchased a Total of 10,000 Tons, Which Would Earn Him Over 400,000 Yuan. How Many Lives of Disaster Victims in Northern Anhui Would This Take? Subsequently, Yang Shucheng Argued That His Authority Was Only to Assist With Transportation Matters. There Were Others Specifically Assigned to This Task. The Person in Charge Was the American Baker. Yu Shaozhen and an American Were in Charge of the Jinpu Road. Moreover, on January 20th, He Was Still in Henan. He Returned to Bengbu on the 21st and Received the Letter of Appointment. He Arrived in Pukou on the 22nd. He Had Absolutely No Connection With the Suspension of Relief Wheat Transportation. Li Shirui Also Presented Baker's Report Published in the Xinwenbao in Mid-May, Stating That Baoxing Factory Wheat Competed With Relief Wheat, Making Transportation Difficult, and That the Difficulties Could Be Reduced if 10,000 Tons of Wheat Were Sold to Baoxing. The Court Immediately Called Baker to Testify. Baker Stated That Yang's Authority Was Indeed Only to Assist and Compete With Transportation. Finally, Both Sides' Lawyers Again Involved the Time Issue. As It Was Necessary to Consult the Case Files, the Court Adjourned. ▲Zha's Statement: Zha Liangzhao, Director of the Emergency Relief Department of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, Hired Three Lawyers, Zhang Shizhao, Yuan Liang, Tang Pengyuan, and Xun to Present a Defense and File a Counter-Suit. Xu Shiying, Guan Jianfan, Li Zhenya, Lu Juewu, Xu Jiashi, Hong Ding, Wang Zhuru, Hu Peiru, Etc., the Original Statement Said That He Was Falsely Accused of Abuse of Power and Breach of Trust by the Legal Representatives of the Anhui Shanghai Fellow-Provincials Association, the Plaintiff in the Self-Lawsuit. He Submits a Defense in Accordance with the Law, Files a Counterclaim, and Submits an Incident Civil Suit. In Recent Years, Liang Zhao Has Been Temporarily Entrusted to Disaster Relief Undertakings in Various Educational Positions in Shaanxi, Gansu, and the Yangtze River Basin. He Has Devoted Himself to His Work for Several Years and Has Prepared for Hardships. This Aspiration Has Not Changed in the Least. Without Guilt, He Can Ask Heaven and Earth. Why Should He Endure False Accusations? Now, the Plaintiffs Do Not Hesitate to Reverse Black and White, Fabricate Facts, and Accuse Him of Unfounded Crimes to Your Court, Confusing the Hearing and Damaging His Reputation. It Is Difficult to Tolerate. In Addition to Submitting a Defense, He Will File a Counterclaim in Accordance with the Law and Include a Civil Suit. He Will Submit the Reasons as Follows. "Defense Section" Zha Argued That the Plaintiffs Disregarded the Facts, Arbitrarily Framed Him, and Did Not Consider the Authority and Responsibilities of the National Government Disaster Relief Committee in Handling Affairs. Instead, They Fabricated Facts Against Individuals. Therefore, None of the Allegations Were Based on Facts, and None Were Fabricated. He Will Now Correct Them Based on Facts. A. The Truth About the Conversion of American Wheat Into Cash. According to the National Government Disaster Relief Committee, in Order to Facilitate Relief Work, It Negotiated With the U.S. Government to Agree to Convert a Portion of the Borrowed American Wheat Into Cash. It Invited Well-Known Figures From Both China and Foreign Countries in Shanghai to Form a Grain Exchange Committee, Collect Public Opinion, and Proceed Publicly. The Process, the Amount of Wheat Sold, and the Funds Were Published in Newspapers and Reported at the General Meeting of the Disaster Relief Committee on June 27 of This Year and Announced to the Public. This Matter Related to the Overall Plan of the Disaster Relief Committee and Was Not Limited to Any Local Disaster Area. Therefore, the Plaintiffs Disregarded the Facts and Issued Implied Words to Confuse the Public Hearing. What Was Their Purpose? It Is Incomprehensible. B. Responsibilities of the Director of the Emergency Relief Department. According to Liang Zhao, He Was the Director of the Emergency Relief Department, but He Was Not a Member of the Grain Exchange Committee. The Plaintiffs Clearly Knew That the Allegations Were Not Within the Scope of the Responsibilities of the Director of the Emergency Relief Department. Therefore, They Insisted That He Was a Member of the Grain Exchange Committee, Thinking That in This Way, They Could Arbitrarily Slander Him. They Did Not Know That One Look at the List of Members of the Grain Exchange Committee Would Reveal That All Chinese and Foreign Members Were Socially Credible and Enthusiastic About Public Welfare. Their Impartial Handling of Affairs Could Not Be Slandered in the Least. Moreover, Liang Zhao Was Not a Member of the Committee. The Plaintiffs Fabricated Facts and Intended to Incriminate People Deliberately. It Only Showed That Their Efforts Were in Vain. It Is So Regrettable. C. The Truth About Signing the Contract. The Contract Between the National Government Disaster Relief Committee and Baoxing Flour Mill to Sell Wheat Was Signed by Vice Chairman Simpson on Behalf of the Committee. There Was the Original Contract as Proof. However, the Plaintiffs Claimed That Liang Zhao "Coerced the First Defendant and Signed the Price Change Contract Up to Three Times," Thinking That They Could Confuse the Public Hearing and Falsely Accuse the Defendant. They Did Not Know That Those Who Signed the Contract on Behalf of the Disaster Relief Committee Were Not Liable. Moreover, Liang Zhao Was Not a Party to Signing the Contract. The Plaintiffs Intended to Subject People to Criminal Penalties and Did Not Hesitate to Reverse Right and Wrong and Fabricate Facts. It Was Truly the Most Ridiculous Thing. "Counterclaim Section" A. Regarding the Criminal Suit Section. Based on the Above Discussion, It Is Known That the Plaintiffs Are Purely Maliciously Framing Him and Fabricating Facts. For the Dignity of the Law, for the Future of Relief Work, and for the Individual's Legal Interests, It Is Difficult to Remain Silent. It Is Requested That Your Court Severely Punish Him in Accordance With the Provisions of Article 180 of the Criminal Law Regarding False Accusations and Articles 325, 330, and 332 Regarding Damage to Reputation. B. Regarding the Civil Suit Section. Since the Plaintiffs Filed a False Accusation Against Liang Zhao, They Have Tried Their Best to Publicize It and Promote It. The Newspapers Are Noisy and Spread North and South. Everyone Is Talking About It. No Matter Old or Young, Liang Zhao's Personal Reputation Has Suffered Tremendous Damage. Even the National Government Disaster Relief Committee and Other Relief Groups and Charitable Organizations Have Been Subject to Slander. It Is Extremely Painful. Therefore, He Will File a Civil Suit in Accordance With the Law, Requesting That the Plaintiffs Be Ordered to Compensate Him 500,000 Yuan for Loss of Reputation. Use Half of the Money to Run Children's Education in the Disaster Area of Northern Anhui and the Other Half to Subsidize Poor Students in Pingjin Schools. (Explanation: Liang Zhao Values Relief Work and Social Reputation Ten Times More Than Life. In the Autumn of the 19th Year of the Republic of China, He Was Kidnapped by Bandits While Providing Relief in Shaanxi. He Was Once Ransomed for 50,000 Yuan. Later, the Bandits Were Kidnapped by Other Bandits. Fortunately, He Was Rescued Without Ransom. The Price of Reputation Is Unlimited and Difficult to Calculate With Money. Moreover, the Spiritual Pain Inflicted on Liang Zhao by the Plaintiffs This Time Is Hundreds of Times Greater Than the Bandits in Shaanxi Hindering Liang Zhao's Physical Freedom. Now, He Will Temporarily Calculate It as Ten Times the Price of the Bandits Ransoming His Life. It Should Be the Above Number and Used to Fill the Just Cause. It Will Also Supplement the Insufficiency of Disaster Relief.) As for All the Losses Suffered Due to the False Accusation This Time, He Should Also Apply to Retain the Right to Claim Compensation in Order to Maintain Legal Interests. Therefore, He Will Urgently Submit a Statement and Report the Facts Truthfully. He Respectfully Asks Your Court to Investigate and Judge Impartially. It Will Be Public Convenience. Respectfully, to the Shanghai First Special District Court. November 22nd, 21st Year of the Republic of China. Huang Diao Invented Tuning Characters ▲Overseas Chinese in Saigon Focus on Phonetics ▲To Go to Beijing Soon to Register With the Ministry Huang Diao, a Cantonese, Has Been Trading in Saigon Since Childhood. He Deeply Feels That the Lack of Uniformity in China's Language Has a Great Impact on the Popularization of Education. Therefore, He Has Focused on Studying Phonetics. He Started With Roman Letters and Studied for More Than Ten Years, but He Could Not Succeed. In the Second Year of the Republic of China, He Changed His Approach and Studied the Book of Changes, Using the Eight Trigrams of Fuxi as a Blueprint. He Developed and Changed Until the Fourteenth Year of the Republic of China, When He Achieved Complete Results. He Also Created a Tuning Dictionary With 7,600 Characters and a Textbook With 4,000 Characters. All the Languages in the World Can Be Spelled, and the Teaching Method Is Also Extremely Simple. The Entire Course Can Be Completed in Six Months. Mr. Huang Is Now 64 Years Old. He Is Deeply Afraid That Heaven Will Not Grant Him Many Years and That It Will Be Lost. Therefore, He Returned to China a Month Ago, Via Hong Kong to Guangzhou. He Has Given Lectures at Zhongshan University. He Recently Came to Shanghai Via Shantou. He Plans to Go to Beijing Soon to Register With the Ministry of Education and Then Establish a School to Teach. Piggy Bank to Save the Country ▲Peacock Company Custom-Made 1,000 to Give to Relatives and Friends ▲Do Not Abandon Words Because of People, Follow Liang Zuoyou's Method Although Liang Zuoyou's Piggy Bank to Save the Country Is Ridiculed by the Chinese People, It Is Not a Good Model for Saving the Country if It Can Be Practiced and Implemented. It Should Not Be Abandoned Because of People's Words. The Peacock Company in This City Established a Piggy Bank to Save the Country Yesterday. It Specially Custom-Made 1,000 Piggy Banks and Distributed Them to Relatives and Friends, Asking Them to Transfer Them to Family Members or Raise Funds From Outside. The Funds Raised Were All Put Into the Piggy Bank. After It Was Full, It Would Be Sent Directly to the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association to Provide Relief to the Volunteer Army. The Group Specially Sent a Representative, You Baiyan, to the Support Association for Contact Yesterday. He Brought Several Piggy Banks Stored With Donations. After the Association Broke Them, It Revealed the Number of Foreign Currencies and Issued Receipts. Riot Police Drove People Away During the Trial of the Yun Case ▲Tu Shanyuan Asked for Punishment and Apology The Yun Huifang Case, a Young Patriot, Was Tried in the Second Branch of the Higher Court of the Public Concession the Other Day. The Police Department Anticipated That There Would Be a Large Number of Spectators That Day, so They Specially Dispatched Chinese and Western Detectives to Prepare Temporarily. That Day, a Western Police Officer Saw That the Spectators Were Very Crowded, Which Hindered Order, So He Used Force to Drive Them Away, Whipping the Audience With His Leather Whip. People Fled in Succession. Tu Shanyuan, Deputy Officer of the Volunteer Army Training Class of the 19th Route Army, Saw This and Was Very Angry. He Protested Against the Western Police Officer Without Success. So Yesterday, He Sent a Letter to the Shanghai Aid Patriotic Patriots Committee, Asking for Reasonable Contact to Achieve the Purpose of Punishing the Murderers and Apologizing. The Letter Said, “Respected Sirs, Yesterday Was the Date for the Appeal Trial of the Yun Huifang Case. Members of This Association and All Citizens Wanted to Understand the Progress of This Case. They All Went to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court to Attend the Hearing. The Court Had Previously Announced That It Would Be Open to the Public, but Temporarily Rejected the Public From the Court. Although There Were Many People, According to the Principle of Public Disclosure, the Participation of the Public Should Be Accommodated as Much as Possible. However, the Court Did Not Do This. Instead, Foreign Bailiffs Instructed Chinese Western Police Officers to Use Force to Drive Away the Public Who Were Rejected From the Court, and Even Used Leather Whips to Beat Them. People, Shanyuan, Were Also One of Those Who Were Insulted at That Time. The Entire Audience Was Forced to Retreat From the Public Court Under the Coercion of Foreign Nationalism. The Concession Court Is Difficult to Restrain by the Agreement, and the Actions of Foreign Police Officers Should Be Subject to the Command of the Chief Officer of the Court to Exercise Their Powers. However, This Time, the Foreign Bailiffs of the Court Instructed Western Police Officers to Take Such Unreasonable Actions Against the Public. Whether It Was Subject to the Order of the Chief Officer, If So, the Court's Use of Power Outside the Law Is Illegal. Otherwise, the Western Police Officer Who Committed the Crime and the Foreign Bailiff Who Instructed the Crime Openly Insulted the Chinese People and Destroyed Our Country's Legal Spirit. They Should Be Subject to Criminal Penalties. Shanyuan's Personal Insult Is a Small Matter, but the Entire National Judicial Organ Was Destroyed by Foreign Police Officers, Which Has a Huge Impact. Therefore, I Specially Submit a Letter to State the Process, Please Contact Your Committee Reasonably, and Be Sure to Achieve the Purpose of Punishing the Murderers and Apologizing. It Is Not Only the Luck of the People in the Concession, but Also the Luck of the Country's Future.” Assassination Attempt by Thugs in Songpan Road ▲Liu Guilin and His Wife Escaped Successfully Liu Guilin, 31 Years Old, From Changzhou, His Wife, Ms. Qian, Works in the Third Cotton Factory. The Couple Went to Their Parents' Home for Dinner Last Night. As It Was Late, They Walked Home. Unexpectedly, When They Reached the Vicinity of Songpan Road in Yangshupu, a Man Came Towards Them, Pulled Out a Handgun, and Fired Two Shots at Their Heads. He Turned Around and Fled. Fortunately, the Couple Escaped Successfully. Only Their Heads Were Grazed by Bullets. Liu Immediately Shouted for Help. The Nearby Police Heard It and Arrived. Seeing That the Murderer Had Escaped, They Sent the Two to the Nearby Sacred Heart Hospital for Treatment. Later, According to Liu, This Murderer Was Acquainted With Him, and Liu Had Introduced Him to a Job. However, At That Time, Liu Had Asked Him for Two Yuan in Sports Fees and Embezzled It. Later, the Murderer Learned About It, but He Did Not Ask About It. Recently, the Murderer's Job Was Stopped. Recalling the Previous Situation, He May Have Been Resentful and Had the Intention. When Asked About the Murderer's Name, He Firmly Refused to Tell. Therefore, the Police Believed That There Were Other Insider Information, So They Have Sent Detectives to Investigate and Arrest the Fugitive Murderer for Interrogation. Taicang War Disaster Relief Association Started Relief The Taicang War Disaster Relief Association Conducted an Emergency Relief Once After the Japanese Troops Withdrew. However, the General Relief Part Was Only Completed After the Investigation Took Time. It Is Said That There Are More Than 20,000 Households. Yesterday (Monday), Relief Began to Be Distributed in the District Offices. It Was Divided Into Three Grades. One Mu or More Received Five Points, Totaling 2 Yuan and 35 Points Per Household. Two Mu or More Received Seven Points, Totaling 3 Yuan and 29 Points. Ten Mu or More Received Nine Points, Totaling 4 Yuan and 23 Points. Municipal Government Announces Management Rules for Food and Beverage Manufacturing Places The Municipal Government of This City Previously Believed That if Various Food and Beverages Manufactured by Food and Beverage Manufacturing Places in the City Were Not Managed, It Would Have a Huge Impact on the Hygiene of Citizens. Therefore, It Ordered the Two Bureaus of Health and Social Affairs to Jointly Draft Provisional Rules for the Management of Food and Beverage Manufacturing Places. The Rules Have Been Drafted and Submitted to the Municipal Government for Approval and Promulgation. The Original Text Is Recorded Below. 1. All Food and Beverage Manufacturing Places Established in This City Should Comply With These Rules to Emphasize Hygiene. 2. All Food and Beverage Manufacturing Places Must Pay a Fee of One Yuan to Apply to the Health Bureau for Inspection. After Approval, Obtain a License With the Seal of the Health Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau. This License Must Be Renewed Once a Year. 3. This License Must Not Be Transferred to Others and Should Be Hung in a Conspicuous Place in the Manufacturing Place. 4. All Manufacturing Places With Attached Retail Departments Should Comply With the City's Rules for the Management of Restaurants. 5. The Construction, Assembly, and Repair of Factory Buildings Must Be Reported in Advance and Conducted According to the Instructions of the Two Bureaus. They Should Also Comply With the Instructions of the Two Bureaus at Any Time to Modify or Add to the Buildings to Make Them Applicable. 6. Spitting Is Prohibited in All Parts of the Factory. The Surroundings of the Factory Must Be Clean. The Workplace and the Place Where Food Is Stored Must Not Be Accommodated or Gathered for Food. Fly-Proofing Equipment Must Be Installed. 7. There Should Be Clean Toilets in the Factory With Screen Windows. Bathrooms Must Be Set Up When Necessary. 8. The Entire Building Should Be Swept and Refreshed on April 10 of Each Year in the Solar Calendar. 9. It Is Not Allowed to Hire or Reside Workers With Infectious Diseases or Skin Diseases. If There Are Illnesses or Deaths, the Health Bureau Must Be Notified Immediately. All Employees in the Factory Must Be Vaccinated by the Health Bureau and Injected With Vaccines to Prevent Cholera and Typhoid. They Must Also Comply With the Instructions to Prevent Various Infectious Diseases. 10. It Is Not Allowed to Adulterate, Impersonate, or Use Toxic Pigments or Unhygienic Raw Materials When Manufacturing Food. Attention Should Be Paid to Cleanliness When Manufacturing. It Is Not Allowed to Use Unclean Water to Mix Raw Materials, and It Is Not Allowed to Use the Mouth to Spray Any Liquid on Food. 11. All Food Delivered for Sale, Such as Bread, Etc., Must Be Wrapped and Stored in Wax Paper or Other Clean Items to Avoid Contamination by Dust, Flies, Etc. 12. The Wrapping Paper for Bread and the Cans and Glass Bottles for Beverages Such as Biscuits, Candies, Soda, and Beer Must Be Approved by the Two Bureaus and Affixed With the Name and Address of the Manufacturing Place and the Exact Weight or Capacity of the Food. 13. All Food Deliverers Must Carry the Current Year's Delivery Voucher Issued by the Two Bureaus. If the Delivery Voucher Is Lost, Etc., The Two Bureaus Should Be Notified Immediately and a Fee of One Yuan Should Be Paid to Hire a New Voucher. 14. All Vehicles Used to Deliver Food Must Be Cleaned and Covered Tightly. It Is Not Allowed to Store Clothes, Bedding, and Other Unclean Items. The Name and Address of the Manufacturing Place Must Be Written on the Vehicles and Equipment. 15. Each Manufacturing Place Must Allow Inspectors From the Health Bureau and the Social Affairs Bureau Wearing Staff Certificates to Check Inside. However, Bribery or Gifts Are Not Allowed. 16. The Health Bureau May Take Samples for Bureau Testing When It Deems It Necessary. However, Receipts Must Be Given Accordingly. If Inferior Products and Unclean Substances Are Found, or If They Are Unsuitable for Consumption, They Will Be Punished. 17. Those Who Violate This Rule Will Be Fined Up to Five Yuan Depending on the Circumstances. Repeated Offenders May Be Fined From Five Yuan to Twenty-Five Yuan and Their Licenses May Be Revoked. 18. These Rules Will Be Implemented After Approval and Promulgation by the Municipal Government. The Trams and Buses at That Location Connect and Run, Sometimes Up to Three Vehicles. Other Vehicles Cannot Overtake Them and Must Wait for Passengers to Get on and Off, Resulting in No Way to Drive Fast. Authors and Publishers Present to the Ministry of Interior to Investigate Piracy The China Authors and Publishers Federation Was Established in July This Year. Shi Zuocai, Director-General of the Federation, Came to Shanghai the Other Day. The Colleagues of the Shanghai Office of the Federation Hosted a Banquet to Welcome Him. This Was Recorded in This Newspaper. Now, the Federation Has Submitted a Document to the Ministry of Interior Regarding the Piracy of Unscrupulous Merchants, Which Said, “Presently, Unscrupulous Merchants of Piracy Are Illegally Profiting. We Request That You Instruct the Provincial Governments of All Provinces to Instruct the Local Public Security Bureaus to Strictly Punish Them in Order to Extend the Rule of Law and Benefit Culture. Publishing Is Originally for the Purpose of Promoting Culture. It Is Not Without Considerable Contribution to the Country and Society. Since the Last 50 Years, Academic Arts and Literature Have Been Changing With Each Passing Day. Talents Have Emerged in Large Numbers. Writings Have Increased. Those Who Learn Either Study Hard and Pass on Knowledge in Books, or Engage in Translation and Introduce Foreigners to the Chinese People. If They Do Not Accumulate Experience and Spend Years, They Cannot Become Writings and Commend Later Generations. Publishers Print and Distribute for Them, or Donate Manuscript Fees or Pay Royalties. They All Have the Intention of Encouraging Learning. From Receiving the Manuscripts to Completing the Books, The Number of People Required for Correction, Proofreading, Typesetting, and Printing Is Large, and the Time Is Not Temporary. The Heavy and Hard Work Is Probably Not Enough for Outsiders to Say. After the Books Are Completed, If There Is No Advertising to Promote Them, There Is No Way to Seek the Knowledge of Readers. If There Are No Intermediate Merchants to Sell Them, There Is No Way to Reach the Hands of Readers. Therefore, the Cost of Paper and Printing for a Book May Seem Very Small, but When Added to the Manuscript Fees and Royalties of the Authors, the Salaries of the Correctors, the Cost of Advertising and Promotion, the Rebates of the Sales Merchants, and the Interest on the Principal Required Before the Book Is Completed, The Number Is Often Several Times That of Paper and Printing. In Books With More Readers and Wider Sales, a Little Profit May Be Gained, but Special Writings With Profound Learning Often Result in Losses. However, Publishers Cannot Be Profitable and Abandon Special Writings, Allowing Them to Be Buried. They Can Only Use What They Earn to Supplement What They Lack, Hoping to Give the Opportunity for Deep Academic Knowledge to Still Be Developed and Promoted. However, There Are Unscrupulous Merchants of Piracy Who Do Not Know What Learning Is. They Only Seek Their Own Private Interests. They Form Gangs to Specialize in Selecting Books With Wider Sales, Secretly Reprinting Them, and Selling Them Openly. The Gourds Are the Same, and the Hai Shi Are Full of Errors. There Are Also Some Literary Villagers and Book Worms Who Borrow the Name of Criticism to Collect the Profits of Piracy. They Even Change the Head and Face, Overturn the Chapters, Falsely Title the Books, and Falsely Accuse the Authors. Readers Do Not Know It, but They Only Know to Be Greedy for the Low Price. They Do Not Have Time to Ask About the Confusion of the Content and the Poor Quality of the Paper and Ink. They Compete to Buy It, Helping Them to Run Rampant. Their Poisonous Stupidity for Learning and Moths for Culture Are Indeed Unpardonable. Although the Country Protects Copyrights and Has Promulgated Special Laws and Regulations on Criminal Penalties, These People Act Like Ghosts, Disregarding Laws and Disciplines. Even if They Are Sometimes Caught, They Are Often Regarded as Minor Matters and Dealt With Lightly. Shallow People Also Echo It From There, Thinking That the Original Version Is Expensive and the Pirated Version Is Cheap, Causing These People to Become More Unscrupulous. They Dare to Collect Huge Funds as a Profession. The Breadth of the Sales Covers All Regions. In the Long Run, Not Only Will Those Who Operate Legitimate Publishing Businesses All Tend to Decline, but Also Those Writers Who Take Learning as Their Profession and Writing as Their Livelihood Will Not Be Able to Survive. Soon, There Will Be No Books to Read in the Market, and Everyone Will Be Unlearned. The Harm to the Country and Society Is Limited. The Unscrupulous Merchants Started Mostly in Beiping. Then They Spread to Various Places. Beiping Repeatedly Cracked Major Piracy Cases. Tianjin and Jinan Also Found Several Cases at the Same Time. They Have All Been Sent to the Local Authorities for Punishment in Accordance With the Law. Recently, It Was Found That Many Bookstores in Major Cities in the Northwest Provinces Display a Lot of Pirated and False Books. These Unscrupulous Merchants Dare to Disregard Laws and Disciplines and Sell Them Openly. If They Are Not Severely Punished, How Can We Warn Against Evil and Guard Against Future Disasters? For This Reason, We Request That Your Ministry Instruct the Provincial Governments of All Provinces to Instruct the Local Public Security Bureaus to Investigate and Punish Them Strictly in Order to Extend the Rule of Law and Benefit Culture. It Is Truly a Public Convenience.” Pudong Electric Company Revises Loan Lighting Installation Method The Pudong Electric Company Has Formulated Loan Lighting Installation Methods to Give Preferential Treatment to Users. Gold Price Rises Again by Five Taels

(The entire city is chaotic and unpredictable) Yesterday, the market saw another hidden upward trend, with considerable volatility, fluctuating rapidly between 760 taels or so. The disordered state made it difficult to grasp the market. The city saw a rise of six taels and one qian, ultimately resulting in a total increase of five taels and two qian. The minds of those in the trade were divided, and withdrawals were irregular. The silver market showed no flexibility, and exchange rates plummeted. Moreover, due to the war-related extension issue and the lack of sympathy from the United States, the price of gold initially surged, soon surpassing the 60-tael mark. However, the overseas situation shifted slightly, with the British pound strong and the US dollar stable, and potentially changing. As a result, the gold price experienced fluctuations of more than two taels mid-day. In the afternoon, due to the Central Bank swapping December for January (swapping 5,600 bars to the Guangdong banks, with a premium of only six taels), the selling pressure was pervasive on the surface, leading to a state of exhaustion, and the price plunged by five taels. Soon after, demand became active because the exchange rate was still stable, regaining strength. Subsequently, it rose above 60 taels again. It is said that the forward trading from the previous day was done at six and a half taels, and in the afternoon, Fuchang acted on behalf of the Central Bank to swap 4,025 bars to Hengxing and 1,575 bars to Yifeng.

(New price of 60 taels appears) From the early opening of January contracts, the price increased by two taels and seven qian, reaching 759 taels and three qian. Large bars did not change, and the price of American silver was nearly stable, not influenced by the decline in exchange rates and American cotton. Then, the price slightly decreased by six or seven qian to eight taels and six qian. Soon after, buying momentum rose, including Yuanheng, Qingfayong, Zhaofengchang, Yuanmao, Hengchangyong, Kangxiang, and Hengyu. Also, because December US dollar trades were at 5625 and Shanghai sold half a yuan to HSBC this month, the price jumped four taels, reaching 62 taels and seven qian. At that time, Huabi offered December half a yuan and January 5625, Yuanmaoyong, Yuantai, Zhaofengchang, Dadecheng, and Hengxing came to sell, immediately reducing the price by over two taels. Around 9:20 AM, it was 60 taels and five qian. It was learned that the order was placed with a half-point spread (125). The US dollar did not change, due to the slight relationship with the exchange rate, the market was flat, from one tael to zero taels and six qian. Subsequently, transactions were sporadic. At 9:45 AM, it was one tael and four qian, Yuhe and Yifengyong sold. Around 10:00 AM, it was 60 taels and four qian. Later, Dadecheng, Futaiheng, Daxingyong, Hengchangyong, Zhaofengchang, Zhifengyong, etc., bought in. In addition, wheat firms absorbed March US dollars at 8125, and January settled at 5625. As December half a yuan was not easily available, the price saw a new price of 62 taels and eight qian. In an instant, Hengxing, Zhaofengchang, Hongli, Wanxing, etc., sold. It was also heard from foreign news that the silver price conference was scheduled for the coming spring. Therefore, confidence faltered, and at 10:30 AM, it was 61 taels and six qian. After a while, it rose by about one tael, and Bingxing, etc., bought in. Around 11:00 AM, Zhaofengchang, Yongfeng, Hengyu, Fuchang, and Yuantai, etc., came to the market to sell, and the price could not be sustained, falling to 60 taels and five qian at 11:30 AM. Afterwards, it stabilized, at one tael and five or six qian. By the noon closing, it was one tael and three qian.

(After selling pressure, it turned upward again) The afternoon market opened at 61 taels and two qian, Yuanchun, Dadecheng, Yifengyong, and Yuanmaoyong bought in, and it immediately rose to 62 taels. At 2:15 PM, it was suddenly rumored that the Central Bank had a large batch of forward contracts, willing to swap out at six taels. Hengyu, Yuanxingyong, Yuhe, and Qianchangxiang, etc., all offered to sell, and at 2:30 PM, it was 58 taels and eight qian. Then, it rose to 60 taels and one qian. However, selling pressure increased, and Dadecheng, Shenkang, Zhifengyong, Yuanmaoyong, Hengyu, and Daxingyong, etc., sold off, mainly because the Central Bank had indeed swapped 5,600 bars to Hengxing and Yifeng, with a premium of only six taels. However, the exchange market was still flat. Until 3:20 PM, it finally reached 56 taels and seven qian. This price was a supplemental quote, with few transactions. Soon, it suddenly turned upward, because wheat firms, etc., absorbed February US dollars at 75, and Yifengyong, Hengyu, Yuanxingyong, Bingxing, Yuanheng, Dadecheng, Yuanmaoyong, Yuantai, etc., took advantage of this to drag in, and the bank absorbed November US dollars at half a yuan, and February traded at 6875. Until 4:20 PM, it was 62 taels and one qian, soon reducing by about one tael. At 4:30 PM, the market closed at 61 taels and eight qian, an increase of five taels and two qian compared to the day before. The daily high was 62 taels and eight qian, and the low was 56 taels and seven qian, a difference of six taels and one qian. The net bar was increased by seventeen taels.

(The listed price was five taels less than before) The listed price was still 820 taels, with a commission of 60 taels to 57 or 8 taels. In the afternoon, it was 58 or 9 taels, then 63 taels, and then 58 taels, which was five taels less than the previous day. The registered price was 68 taels for November, 67 taels for December, and 61 taels for January. The supplemental interest was 67 taels in the morning and 68 taels in the afternoon.

(Various firms had complex and disordered entries and exits) Transactions on the floor were chaotic. Yuanheng, Dadecheng, Xuli, Hengchangyong, Yuankangxiang, Qingfayong, Futaiheng, Richang, Bingxing, and Yuanmao were all buying in. Yuanmaoyong, Zhifengyong, Zhaofengchang, Yuantai, Yifengyong, and Daxingyong were all selling. Hengyu had quite a few entries and exits. In the afternoon, Yuanmaoyong, Yuanheng, Bingxing, Wanxing, Xuli, Yifengyong, Yuantai, Futaiheng, and Zhaofengchang were all buying in. Dadecheng and Hengyu had the most complex withdrawals. Shenkang, Yuhe, Zhifengyong, Hengchangyong, Daxingyong, Changshengyong, and Yongfeng were all selling. The Dalian banks bought a total of 500 bars and sold 200 bars. The Guangdong banks bought and sold only 300 bars. Hedging transactions were trivial and complex.

Foreign Exchange Market Conditions Are Inconsistent

(British Loose...American Tight)

Yesterday, the silver market reported flat, and the exchange rate continued to fall by more than one cent. This led to differences in local exchange rates. HSBC listed the British pound long at 125, and the US dollar unchanged. Other currencies such as the Indian rupee, French franc, Dutch guilder, and Singapore dollar were also cheaper. Only the German mark slightly decreased by 25. Hong Kong was as before, and the domestic market also showed a trend of British loose and American tight. The British pound initially weakened, then stabilized, with transactions of 100,000 pounds. Sassoon sold slightly, and gold banks were slightly filled. As a result, the price was longer by zero point zero six two five compared to the previous day. The US dollar was initially flat, then firm, then weakened, with slight fluctuations in the afternoon. Ultimately, it was shorter by zero point zero six two five compared to the previous day. In the gold industry, the front market was dug up and filled, and the back market continued to sell. Various banks, including Huabi, sold some. Old Citibank and Macgarry were all absorbing positions. Meifeng once made British and American exchange rates (December), with the US dollar at 29.5625, and received shillings at 6875, equivalent to 3.27 US dollars. "Foreign" Market Is Quite Prosperous, "Silver" Collection Is Weak

Yesterday, the financial situation was such that only foreign transactions were active. Due to strong customer sales, there was fierce competition to buy in the market, which in turn made sellers reluctant to sell, waiting for a good price. Thus, the situation gradually tightened, and banks were deliberately seeking to secure the resource with all their might. Therefore, the market sentiment was very strong, and prices frequently reached new levels. The silver market, on the other hand, remained loose and weak. It is feared that in the near future, it will not recover to a high level.

(Interest Rates Rose to New Levels, Discounting Softened) The early market interest rate for "foreign interest" was one hao and two hu and a half higher than the previous afternoon, at 7 qian, 1 fen, and 2 li. The afternoon market continued to rise by one li and two hao and a half, to 7 qian, 1 fen, and 3 li and 2 hao. As a result, it rose by a huge one li and seven hao and a half compared to the previous day's early market. The early and noon markets for "silver discounts" both opened at two fen, which was one fen less than the previous day. The initial premium for checks plus water was two or three fen, then immediately white checks, and finally there were still one or two fen on the market.

(Guangjiao Followed the Increase Due to the Interest Rate Rise) The early market price for "Jiangnan" small foreign silver was 6 qian, 1 fen, and 7 li and a half, which was one li and a half higher than the previous day's early market. The noon market price was the same, with 5,500 jiao transacted in the early market and 3,000 jiao in the noon market. "Guangdong" small foreign silver did not rise or fall in Japan yesterday, but then followed the interest rate rise and increased by one li, with the early market at 6 qian, 1 fen, and 5 li and a half, and the noon market at 6 qian, 1 fen, and 6 li and a half. 115,000 jiao were transacted in the early market and 45,000 jiao in the noon market. "Copper coins" shortened by 1,000 wen, to 396,500,000 wen, with 36,081,500,000 wen transacted, equivalent to 9,100 taels of silver.

(Silver and Foreign Currency Inflows and Outflows Are Strong and Weak) "Silver currency" bank collections were much weaker compared to the previous day. Chinese merchant collection notes were only over 2.2 million, foreign merchant collection notes were over 1.9 million, special collection notes were 2.45 million, various cargo exchange tax miscellaneous collections were 7.56 million, deposit transactions were 1.34 million, warehouse releases were 1.1 million, money shop silver public notes collections were over 32 million, check collections were over 4.4 million, various route exchange collections were over 800,000, and cash collections were 890,000. Off-market banknotes were 95,000 in the early market and 85,000 in the noon market. Checks were 60,000 in the early market and 70,000 in the noon market. Securities and Bond Prices Rose Sharply Again Yesterday

(Good for five or six jiao to one yuan and three or four jiao)

(Transactions reached more than 10.06 million yuan)

Yesterday (22nd), the market conditions of various bonds in the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange, the futures market rose quite sharply again, the market buying and selling sentiment continued to be more active than before, and the situations between various markets were very lively. The statistics show that the turnover was far better than the previous day. Although there were many kinds of spot transactions, the turnover was still rare. Although there has been no major development in the overall situation, the general situation is indeed better than before. The Lu case has been resolved, and the Shu case will not expand. The domestic situation is indeed optimistic. Therefore, the market sentiment has always been good, and investments from all parties are more active than sales. The price has been rising steadily, much higher than a few months ago. Yesterday's sharp rise in various prices was still due to the approaching delivery date and the strong demand. It was found that the financial industry has also successively increased its holdings recently, and they are all investments, which has a great impact on the market. It is estimated that yesterday, except for the entire Six Customs Tax and the 20-roll current month, which only gained five or six jiao, the rest rose by one yuan to one yuan and three or four jiao. According to statistics, the total spot transactions for the day were 14,000 yuan, the futures were more than 5.6 million in the morning, and more than 5 million in the afternoon, totaling 10,066,000 yuan.

Cotton Yarn Market Under Heavy Pressure

(Sellers Have Ample Chips in Hand)

The cotton yarn market has softened, the situation is calm, but customer sales are still sluggish, and all banks are inactive. The overseas trend of American cotton continues to fall, causing a lack of confidence. Some are adopting a wait-and-see attitude due to thin bottom plates. However, sellers have ample chips in hand, so the pressure is still heavy.

(Manpower Indicator Softened) At the opening of the previous market manpower indicator, the market softened due to the further decline in American cotton. Each month fell by 1, 2, or 3 qian. The market became weaker in the afternoon, and the downward trend intensified, with each month falling by 3, 4, 5, or 7 qian. The total turnover for the day was 33,400 bales. Total Long sold 1,400 bales, Mingde 1,800 bales, Tongxing 1,550 bales, Dachangcheng 1,200 bales, and Tonghe 1,300 bales. Dafeng bought 1,700 bales, Changfeng 2,630 bales, Shenji 1,550 bales, Yichang 1,200 bales, Jifeng 900 bales, and Dachang 900 bales. The closing prices are listed below:

More New Sellers in the Cotton Market

The cotton market has turned soft again. Because American cotton has fallen continuously and the yarn market has no upward momentum, this has caused profit-takers to close out their positions, and there are more new sellers. The market has rapidly turned downstream. However, a certain manufacturer still bought in this month to抵空 (offset shorts). In the afternoon, the market mostly said that a certain household had 4,000 dans of goods received in October, which have now been delivered. Therefore, the situation is becoming weaker and weaker, but there are still few sources from various routes. It is feared that there will be no large-scale decline in the future. However, the situation of American cotton is still not good, and it is restrained by it.

(Zheng Standard Turns Downstream) At the opening of the Zheng Standard market, the market selling sentiment was strong due to the further decline in American cotton. Each month fell by 2 or 3 qian. In the afternoon, it fell by another 1 and a half qian. The total turnover for the day was 103,300 dans. Rongxing sold 3,000 dans, Shenchang 1,900 dans, Dachangcheng 2,100 dans, Ruiyuan 2,400 dans, Yuantai 2,300 dans, and Changfeng 2,800 dans.
